#Create a simulator object
set ns [new Simulator]

#Define different colors for data flows (for NAM)
$ns color 1 Red
$ns color 2 Blue
$ns color 3 Green
$ns color 4 Yellow
$ns color 5 Black

#Open the NAM trace file
set nf [open /home/lucas/Documents/ns2/nsOutput/afterupload100_scriptNS2_0416802013.nam w]
$ns namtrace-all $nf

#Define a 'finish' procedure
proc finish {} {
	global ns nf
	$ns flush-trace
	#Close the NAM trace file
	close $nf
	exit 0
}

#Server Moodle
set internet [$ns node]
set server [$ns node]
$ns duplex-link $internet $server 100Mb 60ms DropTail

#Create connection TCP Polo 1


#Polo 1 Maquina 1 -- Servidor
set tcpP1M1ToServer [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpP1M1ToServer set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $P1M1 $tcpP1M1ToServer
set sinkP1M1ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP1M1ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP1M1ToServer $sinkP1M1ToServer
$tcpP1M1ToServer set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP1M1ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP1M1ToServer attach-agent $tcpP1M1ToServer
$ftpP1M1ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 1 Maquina 1
set tcpServerToP1M1 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP1M1 set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP1M1
set sinkServerToP1M1 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P1M1 $sinkServerToP1M1
$ns connect $tcpServerToP1M1 $sinkServerToP1M1
$tcpServerToP1M1 set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP1M1 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP1M1 attach-agent $tcpServerToP1M1
$ftpServerToP1M1 set type_ FTP

set tcpServerToP1M4 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP1M4 set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP1M4
set sinkServerToP1M4 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P1M4 $sinkServerToP1M4
$ns connect $tcpServerToP1M4 $sinkServerToP1M4
$tcpServerToP1M4 set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP1M4 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP1M4 attach-agent $tcpServerToP1M4
$ftpServerToP1M4 set type_ FTP

$ftpP1M24ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 1 Maquina 24
set tcpServerToP1M24 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP1M24 set class_ 1
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP1M24
set sinkServerToP1M24 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P1M24 $sinkServerToP1M24
$ns connect $tcpServerToP1M24 $sinkServerToP1M24
$tcpServerToP1M24 set fid_ 1
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP1M24 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP1M24 attach-agent $tcpServerToP1M24
$ftpServerToP1M24 set type_ FTP

set ftpP2M14ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP2M14ToServer attach-agent $tcpP2M14ToServer
$ftpP2M14ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 2 Maquina 14
set tcpServerToP2M14 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP2M14 set class_ 2
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP2M14
set sinkServerToP2M14 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P2M14 $sinkServerToP2M14
$ns connect $tcpServerToP2M14 $sinkServerToP2M14

$ns attach-agent $P4M7 $tcpP4M7ToServer
set sinkP4M7ToServer [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $server $sinkP4M7ToServer
$ns connect $tcpP4M7ToServer $sinkP4M7ToServer
$tcpP4M7ToServer set fid_ 4
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP4M7ToServer [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP4M7ToServer attach-agent $tcpP4M7ToServer
$ftpP4M7ToServer set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 4 Maquina 7
set tcpServerToP4M7 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpServerToP4M7 set class_ 4
$ns attach-agent $server $tcpServerToP4M7
set sinkServerToP4M7 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P4M7 $sinkServerToP4M7
$ns connect $tcpServerToP4M7 $sinkServerToP4M7

#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpServerToP4M7 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpServerToP4M7 attach-agent $tcpServerToP4M7
$ftpServerToP4M7 set type_ FTP

$ftpServerToP5M16 attach-agent $tcpServerToP5M16
$ftpServerToP5M16 set type_ FTP

$ftpLS1ToP1M5 attach-agent $tcpLS1ToP1M5
$ftpLS1ToP1M5 set type_ FTP

$ftpP5M4ToLS5 set type_ FTP
#Server -- Polo 5 Maquina 4
set tcpLS5ToP5M4 [new Agent/TCP]
$tcpLS5ToP5M4 set class_ 5
$ns attach-agent $P5LS $tcpLS5ToP5M4
set sinkLS5ToP5M4 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P5M4 $sinkLS5ToP5M4
$ns connect $tcpLS5ToP5M4 $sinkLS5ToP5M4
$tcpLS5ToP5M4 set fid_ 5
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpLS5ToP5M4 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpLS5ToP5M4 attach-agent $tcpLS5ToP5M4
$ftpLS5ToP5M4 set type_ FTP

$ns attach-agent $P5M23 $tcpP5M23ToLS5
set sinkP5M23ToLS5 [new Agent/TCPSink]
$ns attach-agent $P5LS $sinkP5M23ToLS5
$ns connect $tcpP5M23ToLS5 $sinkP5M23ToLS5
$tcpP5M23ToLS5 set fid_ 5
#Configurando uma aplicacao FTP para o TCP
set ftpP5M23ToLS5 [new Application/FTP]
$ftpP5M23ToLS5 attach-agent $tcpP5M23ToLS5
$ftpP5M23ToLS5 set type_ FTP
